		<script type="text/javascript">
			function bodyonload() { 
				
	ViewInventory.setSearchYears(document.forms.SavedSearchFilter); 
	
	
	
		loadClasses(document.forms.SavedSearchFilter);
		loadMakes(document.forms.SavedSearchFilter);
		loadBodyStyles(document.forms.SavedSearchFilter); 
	
	ViewInventory.setModelTitles(document.forms.SavedSearchFilter);
	
	/* Add change handler to each select to update the Search Name */
	$$('#SavedSearchFilter select').each(function(elm){
		elm.observe('change',updateSearchName);
	});
 
			}
		</script>
	


	<script type="text/javascript">
		getCurrentInventoryAlerts = function() {
			new Ajax.Updater('current_alerts','/index.cfm?fuseaction=viewinventory.currentalerts&ajax=true',{ asynchronous: true, evalScripts: true });
		}
		
		SavedSearchValidate = function(f) {
			f.searchname.value = f.searchname.value.replace(/^\s*(.*?)\s*$/,'$1');
			if (f.searchname.length==0) {
				alert('Please name this search.');
				f.searchname.select(); return false;
			}
			
			if (typeof f.Email != 'undefined') {
				if(validateEmail(f.Email.value) != true) {
					alert('Please enter a valid email address.');
					f.Email.select();
					return false;
				}
			}
			
			// fetch criteria from the search form
			var select = null;
			var input = null;
			var filter = $('SavedSearchFilter');
			for (var i = 0; i < filter.length; i++) {
				select = filter.elements[i];
				input = eval('f.' + select.name.toLowerCase());
				if (select.tagName.toLowerCase() == 'select'
						&& select.selectedIndex >= 0
						&& typeof input != 'undefined') {
					input.value = select.options[select.selectedIndex].value;
				}
			}
			
			if(filter.Awning)
				f.awning.value = (filter.Awning.checked==true)? 1: 0;
			if(filter.Generator)
				f.generator.value = (filter.Generator.checked==true)? 1: 0;
			
			dpPopup(f.action + '?' + Form.serialize(f) + '&ajax=true&suppressLayout=true','SearchSaved','Thank You!',300,200).center();
			return false;
		}
		
		updateSearchName = function() {
			var f = $('SavedSearchFilter');
			var save = document.forms.frmInvAlert;
			var name = '';
			
			function getLabel(input) {
				with (input) {
					return (options.length > 1 && selectedIndex >= 0 && options[selectedIndex].value != '')? options[selectedIndex].innerHTML: '';
				}
			}
			name += getLabel(f.Car_TypeID) + ' ';
			
			var startyear = getLabel(f.YearStart);
			var endyear = getLabel(f.YearEnd);
			if (startyear==endyear) { name += startyear + ' '; }
			if(f.Car_HullMaterialID)
				name += getLabel(f.Car_HullMaterialID) + ' ';
			name += getLabel(f.Car_MakeID) + ' ';
			name += getLabel(f.Car_ModelID) + ' ';
			name += getLabel(f.Car_BodyStyleID) + ' ';

			var minprice = getLabel(f.PriceStart).replace(/ /,"");
			var maxprice = getLabel(f.PriceEnd).replace(/ /,"");
			if (minprice.length!=0 && maxprice.length!=0) { name += minprice + ' to ' + maxprice + ' '; }
			else if (minprice.length!=0) { name += 'over ' + minprice + ' '; }
			else if (maxprice.length!=0) { name += 'under ' + maxprice + ' '; }
			save.searchname.value = name.replace(/\s+/g,' ').replace(/\s+$/,'').replace(/ \([0-9]+\)/g,'');
		}
	</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
		highlightSearchTab = function(a) {
				ViewInventory.closeVehicleWindow();
				var tabs = $('search_tabsethead').getElementsByTagName('a');
				for (i = 0; i < tabs.length; i++) {
					tabs[i].className = '';
					$(tabs[i].getAttribute('tab')).style.display = 'none';
				}
				$$('.list_tab').each(function(t){
				    t.remove()
				});
			if (a != '') {
				a.className = 'selected';
				$(a.getAttribute('tab')).style.display = 'block';
			}
		};

		getSelectedTab = function() {
			var tabs = $('search_tabsethead').getElementsByTagName('a');
			for (var i = 0; i < tabs.length; i++) {
				if (tabs[i].className == 'selected') { return $(tabs[i].getAttribute('tab')); }
			} return '';
		};

		getCarClass = function() {
			var f = $('InventorySearch');
			var c = f.Car_ClassID;
			if (c.tagName == 'select') {
				switch (c.options.length) {
					case 0: { return f.JSClassID.value; }
					case 1: { return c.options[1].value; }
					default: { return c.options[Math.max(c.selectedIndex,1)].value; }
				}
			} else {
				return $j('input[name=Car_ClassID]:checked').length > 0 ? $j('input[name=Car_ClassID]:checked:first').attr('value') : $j('input[name=Car_ClassID]:first').attr('value');	
			}
		};

		getSearchTab = function(id,car_classid) {
			var tabs = $('search_tabsethead').getElementsByTagName('a');
			if (car_classid==null) { car_classid = getCarClass(); }
			for (var i = 0; i < tabs.length; i++) {
				if (tabs[i].getAttribute('tab') == id && (id != 'search_results' ||
				(id == 'search_results' && tabs[i].getAttribute('car_classid') == car_classid))) { return tabs[i]; }
			} return '';
		};
		
		setSearchTab = function(a,reload) {
			a = (typeof a == 'string')? getSearchTab(a): a;
			
			if (typeof a == 'string') {
				a = $('search_tabsethead').getElementsByTagName('a')[0];
			}
			
			if (reload==true || a.className!='selected') {
				
				var invSearch = $('InventorySearch');
				$('savedsearchdescription').hide();
				$('savedsearchform_container').hide();
				$('searchform_container').show();
				
				highlightSearchTab(a); var i = 0;
				var tab = $(a.getAttribute('tab'));
				
				switch (tab.id) {
					case 'savedsearch': {
						var filters = invSearch.serialize().split('&');
						var save = $('frmInvAlert');
						var param = null;

						$('searchform_container').hide();
						
						$('savedsearchdescription').show();
						$('savedsearchform_container').show();
						if (typeof $('search-summary') != 'undefined' && $('search-summary')) {
							$('search-summary').hide();
						}

						updateSearchName();
						for (i = 0; i < filters.length; i++) {
							param = filters[i].split('=');
							if (param.length==2 && param[0].toLowerCase()!='fuseaction'
									&& typeof save[param[0]]!='undefined' && save[param[0]].type && save[param[0]].type=='hidden') {
								save[param[0]].value=param[1];
							}
						}
						break;
					}
					case 'fulldetail': { break; }
					case 'webspecials': {
						if (typeof $('search-summary') != 'undefined' && $('search-summary')) {
							$('search-summary').show();
						}
						if (reload != false) {
							ViewInventory.submitInventorySearch({active_webspecial:1},true);
						}
						break;
					}
					case 'search_results': {
						var car_class = a.getAttribute('car_classid');
						if (typeof $('search-summary') != 'undefined' && $('search-summary')) {
							$('search-summary').show();
						}
						with (invSearch.Car_ClassID) {
							if (typeof selectedIndex != 'undefined' && selectedIndex >= 0 && car_class != options[selectedIndex].value) {
								// setting the container class controls
								// show/hide of form elements related to
								// different vehicle classes such as boats or RVs
								$('searchfilter_container').className = 'carclass' + car_class;
								var more = form.ShowMoreOptions.checked;
								form.reset(); form.ShowMoreOptions.checked = more;
								for (i=0; i < options.length; i++) {
									if (options[i].value==car_class) { options[i].selected = true; }
								}
								loadInventoryMakes(form);
							}
						}
						
						if (reload != false) {
							ViewInventory.submitInventorySearch({active_webspecial:0},true);
						}
					}
				}
			}
			return false;
		};

		viewAllInventory = function(specials,classid) {
			var frm = $('InventorySearch');
			if (specials == null) { specials = frm.active_webspecial.checked; }
			if (classid == null) {
				with (frm.Car_ClassID) {
					if (typeof tagName != 'undefined' && tagName == 'select') {
						classid = (selectedIndex <= 0) ? f.JSClassID.value : options[selectedIndex].value;
					} else {
						/* stop torturing myself and just use jquery! */
						classid = $j('input[name=Car_ClassID]:checked').length > 0 ? $j('input[name=Car_ClassID]:checked:first').attr('value') : $j('input[name=Car_ClassID]:first').attr('value');
					}
				}
			}
			var more = (typeof frm.ShowMoreOptions != 'undefined' && frm.ShowMoreOptions.checked)? frm.ShowMoreOptions.value: 0;
			var tab = (specials==true)? 'webspecials' : 'search_results';
			var ws = (specials==true)?1:0;
			/* reset filters */
			if (typeof $('search-summary') != 'undefined' && $('search-summary')) {
				_InventoryAdvancedSearch.reset();
			} else {
				frm.reset();
			}
			
			
			/* reset alert */
			$j('#resultAlertBlock').hide();
			if (specials == true) {
				
					
					if(typeof frm.Car_TypeID != 'undefined'){
						frm.Car_TypeID.value = '';
					}
				
			} else {
				if (typeof frm.Car_FuelID != 'undefined') {
					frm.Car_FuelID.value = '';
				}
				if (typeof frm.certpreowned != 'undefined') {
					frm.certpreowned.value = '';
				}
			}
			
			setSearchTab(tab,false);
			ViewInventory.submitInventorySearch({ Car_ClassID:classid, ShowMoreOptions:more, active_webspecial:ws });
			return false;
		};

		getSearchPage = function(url) {
			url += '&ajax=true';
			var set = {startrow:url.replace(/^.*[?&]startrow=(\d*).*$/gi,'$1')};
			var rpp = url.replace(/^.*[?&]maxrows=(\d*).*$/gi,'$1');
			if (isNaN(parseInt(rpp))==false) { set.maxrows = rpp; }
			ViewInventory.submitInventorySearch(set);
			$('search_tabsethead').scrollTo();
		};
	</script>

<h1><small>Hubler Auto Group - Indianapolis, Shelbyville, Bedford, Rushville, Greenwood, Franklin IN</small></h1>
<p style="text-align: left;"><br>

 <span style="font-size: 10pt;">Hubler Automotive Group has been servicing Indianapolis and the surrounding area for many years with a strong commitment to our community and to great customer service. We treat the needs of each individual customer with paramount concern. We know that you have high expectations, and as a car dealer we enjoy the challenge of meeting and exceeding those standards each and every time. Our showrooms are worth the short drive from Franklin, Greenwood, or anywhere else in Indiana. Come experience our commitment to excellence for yourself!</span><br>

 <span style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>

 Our experienced sales staff is eager to share its knowledge and enthusiasm with you. We encourage you to browse our online inventory, schedule a test drive and investigate <span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;"><strong><a href="http://www.drivehubler.com/financing" target="_blank">financing options</a></strong></span>.</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>

 When it comes to a high quality, competitively priced <strong><a href="http://www.drivehubler.com/used-cars/for-sale" target="_blank">used vehicles</a></strong> in the Indianapolis IN area, Hubler Automotive Group is your destination. We strive to maintain a huge selection of used cars by today&#39;s top auto manufacturers. You can get a <strong><a href="http://www.drivehubler.com/used-cars/for-sale" target="_blank">used car</a></strong> that has been through a detailed inspection by our auto technicians and will run like new for many years to come.</span><br>

 <span style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>

 Want a loan with a low payment? How about a short-term loan that will have your vehicle paid off in just a few years? Have bad credit? Come to any of our Hubler dealerships and speak to one of our financial experts. We&#39;ll create a loan program tailored to your needs to ensure you can afford to drive away with one of our new or used vehicles. 	function getLocation(currSeller){

		var currLocation;
	
	switch(currSeller){

		case "Hubler Acura":
		currLocation = '4917201';
		break;		
		
		case "Hubler Outlet Center":
		currLocation = '4917208';
		break;
				
		case "Hubler Bedford":
		currLocation = '4917202';
		break;

		case "Bradley Chevrolet":
		currLocation = '4917203';
		break;
				
		case "Hubler Chevrolet":
		currLocation = '4917204';
		break;	
			
		case "Hubler Ford":
		currLocation = '4917205';
		break;	
			
		case "Hubler Mazda":
		currLocation = '4917206';
		break;	
			
		case "Hubler Nissan":
		currLocation = '4917207';
		break;
				
		case "Hubler Auto Center":
		currLocation = '4917209';
		break;	
			
		case "Hubler Chevrolet Center":
		currLocation = '4917211';
		break;  
  		
		default:
		  currLocation = '';
		}

		return currLocation;


	}
});
